                    {unit.isSpecial && <div className="absolute top-0 left-0 bg-[#c5a059] text-white text-xs px-3 py-1 rounded-br-lg z-10">ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖҰГҷЕ ГҳВІГҳВ©</div>}
                    {unit.isSold && (
                      <div className="absolute inset-0 z-20 flex items-center justify-center bg-white/50 backdrop-blur-[1px] pointer-events-none">
                        <div className="border-[5px] border-red-600 text-red-600 text-3xl font-black px-6 py-2 rounded-xl transform -rotate-12 opacity-80 shadow-lg tracking-wider">ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВЁГҷЕ ГҳВ№ / ГҷвҖҰГҳВӯГҳВ¬ГҷЛҶГҳВІ</div>
                      </div>
                    )}
                    <div className="p-5 cursor-pointer" onClick={() => toggleUnit(unit.id)}>
                      <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                        <div>
                          <span className="block font-bold text-xl text-[#1a365d]">{unit.title}</span>
                          <span className="text-[#c5a059] font-black text-lg">{unit.price}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div className="flex flex-col items-end gap-2 mt-2">
                          <span className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-bold ${unit.isSpecial ? "bg-[#c5a059]/10 text-[#c5a059]" : "bg-slate-100 text-slate-600"}`}>{unit.badge}</span>
                          <ChevronDown className={`text-slate-400 transition-transform duration-300 mt-1 ${expandedUnit === unit.id ? "rotate-180" : ""}`} />
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    {expandedUnit === unit.id && (
                      <div className="px-5 pb-5 bg-slate-50/50 border-t border-slate-100 pt-4 animate-fadeIn">
                        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 text-sm text-slate-600 mb-6">
                          <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Ruler size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> {unit.roof ? "422 ГҷвҖҰГӮВІ" : "204 ГҷвҖҰГӮВІ"}</span>
                          <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Bed size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> {unit.roof ? "4 ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒ" : "5 ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒ"}</span>
                          <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><UserCheck size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒГҳВ© ГҳВ®ГҳВ§ГҳВҜГҷвҖҰГҳВ©</span>
                          <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Droplets size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒГҳВ© ГҳВәГҳВіГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ</span>
                          {!unit.roof && <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Fingerprint size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҳВҜГҳВ®ГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ ГҳВ°ГҷЖ’ГҷЕ </span>}
                          {!unit.roof && <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Wifi size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖ ГҳВІГҷвҖһ ГҳВ°ГҷЖ’ГҷЕ </span>}
                          {unit.roof && <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Umbrella size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҳВіГҳВ·ГҳВӯ ГҳВ®ГҳВ§ГҳВө ГҷЖ’ГҳВЁГҷЕ ГҳВұ</span>}
                          {!unit.roof && <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Box size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҷвҖҰГҳВіГҳВӘГҷЛҶГҳВҜГҳВ№</span>}
                          {!unit.roof && <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Car size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҷвҖҡГҷВҒ ГҳВ®ГҳВ§ГҳВө</span>}
                          <span className="col-span-2 flex items-center gap-2"><Layers size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҳВ®ГҳВІГҳВ§ГҷвҖ  ГҳВЈГҳВұГҳВ¶ГҷЕ  ГҷЛҶГҳВ№ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҷЕ  ГҷвҖҰГҳВіГҳВӘГҷвҖҡГҷвҖһ</span>
                          <span className="col-span-2 flex items-center gap-2"><Bath size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> 4 ГҳВҜГҷЛҶГҳВұГҳВ§ГҳВӘ ГҷвҖҰГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖЎ</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        {/* ГҳВЈГҳВІГҳВұГҳВ§ГҳВұ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӯГҳВ¬ГҳВІ ГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВӘГҳВөГҳВ§ГҷвҖһ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ¬ГҳВҜГҷЕ ГҳВҜГҳВ© */}
                        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 pt-4 border-t border-slate-200 relative z-30">
                          <button 
                            onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); window.scrollTo(0, 0); navigate('/contact'); }} 
                            disabled={unit.isSold}
                            className={`flex-1 py-3 rounded-xl text-sm font-bold transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2 ${unit.isSold ? 'bg-slate-200 text-slate-400 cursor-not-allowed' : 'bg-[#1a365d] text-white hover:bg-[#c5a059] shadow-md'}`}
                          >
                            <CalendarCheck size={18} /> {unit.isSold ? "ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҳВӯГҳВҜГҳВ© ГҳВәГҷЕ ГҳВұ ГҷвҖҰГҳВӘГҳВ§ГҳВӯГҳВ©" : "ГҳВ§ГҳВӯГҳВ¬ГҳВІ ГҷвҖЎГҳВ°ГҷвҖЎ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҳВӯГҳВҜГҳВ©"}
                          </button>
                          <a 
                            href="tel:920032842" 
                            onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
                            className="flex-1 bg-white border-2 border-[#1a365d] text-[#1a365d] py-3 rounded-xl text-sm font-bold hover:bg-slate-50 transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2 shadow-sm"
                          >
                            <PhoneCall size={18} /> 920032842
                          </a>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
          <div className="order-1 lg:order-2 h-full min-h-[400px]">
            <div className="relative group cursor-pointer overflow-hidden rounded-3xl shadow-lg border-4 border-white h-full bg-slate-200 flex items-center justify-center" onClick={() => setPreviewImg(images[selectedFloor])}>
              <div className="absolute top-4 left-4 z-20 w-16 h-16 md:w-24 md:h-24 opacity-50 pointer-events-none mix-blend-multiply">
                <img src={getImg("1I5KIPkeuwJ0CawpWJLpiHdmofSKLQglN")} className="w-full h-full object-contain" alt="Logo" />
              </div>
              <img src={images[selectedFloor]} className="w-full h-full object-cover transform group-hover:scale-105 transition duration-700" alt="ГҷвҖҰГҳВ®ГҳВ·ГҳВ·" />
              <div className="absolute bottom-6 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 bg-white/90 backdrop-blur px-6 py-3 rounded-full text-sm font-bold text-[#1a365d] shadow-lg flex items-center gap-2 transition-transform hover:scale-105">
                <ZoomIn size={16} /> ГҳВ§ГҳВ¶ГҳВәГҳВ· ГҷвҖһГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҷЖ’ГҳВЁГҷЕ ГҳВұ
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

const ToastNotification = () => {
  const { toast } = useContext(AppContext);
  return (
    <div className={`fixed bottom-10 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-[100] bg-white border-r-4 ${toast.type === "error" ? "border-red-500" : "border-[#c5a059]"} px-8 py-4 rounded-xl shadow-2xl flex items-center gap-4 transition-all duration-500 no-print ${toast.show ? "translate-y-0 opacity-100 visible" : "translate-y-20 opacity-0 invisible"}`}>
      <div className={`p-2 rounded-full ${toast.type === "error" ? "bg-red-100 text-red-600" : "bg-green-100 text-green-600"}`}>
        <CircleCheckBig size={24} />
      </div>
      <div>
        <p className="font-bold text-[#1a365d]">{toast.title}</p>
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">{toast.desc}</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const MainApp = () => {
  // Г°ЕёвҖқВҘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВ№ГҳВҜГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ ГҷвҖЎГҷвҖ ГҳВ§: ГҳВӘГҳВ№ГҷЕ ГҷЕ ГҷвҖ  ГҳВ§ГҳВіГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҷвҖҡГҳВ№ ГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҙГҳВ№ГҳВ§ГҳВұ ГҷВҒГҷЕ  ГҳВӘГҳВЁГҷЛҶГҷЕ ГҳВЁ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВӘГҳВөГҷВҒГҳВӯ
  useEffect(() => {
    document.title = "ГҳВіГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҷЖ’ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҡГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВ© | ГҳВіГҷвҖҡГҷВҒ ГҷЕ ГҳВ№ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶ ГҳВЁГҳВұГҳВӨГҷЕ ГҳВӘГҷЖ’ГҳЕ’ ГҷЛҶГҷвҖҰГҳВіГҷЖ’ГҷвҖ  ГҷЕ ГҳВӯГҷЖ’ГҷЕ  ГҷвҖҡГҳВөГҳВӘГҷЖ’";
    let icon = document.querySelector("link[rel~='icon']");
    if (!icon) {
      icon = document.createElement("link");
      icon.rel = "icon";
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(icon);
    }
    // ГҷЛҶГҳВ¶ГҳВ№ГҷвҖ ГҳВ§ ГҷвҖҰГҳВ№ГҳВұГҷвҖҳГҷВҒ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВөГҷЛҶГҳВұГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ®ГҳВ§ГҳВө ГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҙГҳВ№ГҳВ§ГҳВұ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВөГҳВәГҳВұ
    icon.href = getImg("1CcCFvgasNW1MEZt65AY9ZD7FzdDvuNgJ", "w128");
  }, []);

  return (
    <Router>
      <div dir="rtl" className="min-h-screen flex flex-col font-cairo text-slate-900 bg-slate-50">
        
        <GlobalStyles />
        <ToastNotification />
        <Navbar />

        <div className="flex-grow pt-24">
          <Routes>
            {/* ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВөГҷВҒГҳВӯГҳВ§ГҳВӘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰГҳВ© */}
            <Route path="/" element={<Home />} />
            <Route path="/about" element={<About />} />
            <Route path="/projects" element={<Projects />} />
            <Route path="/contact" element={<Contact />} />
            <Route path="/handover" element={<UnitHandover />} />
            <Route path="/privacy" element={<LegalPage title="ГҳВіГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҳВіГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ®ГҳВөГҷЛҶГҳВөГҷЕ ГҳВ©" />} />
            <Route path="/terms" element={<LegalPage title="ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҙГҳВұГҷЛҶГҳВ· ГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВЈГҳВӯГҷЖ’ГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰ" />} />
            <Route path="/inspection" element={<UnitInspection />} />
            
            {/* ГҳВЁГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҳВЁГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВЎ */}
            <Route path="/customer-login" element={<CustomerLogin />} />
            <Route path="/maintenance" element={<Maintenance />} />

            {/* ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҳВӯГҳВ§ГҳВӘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВӯГҷЖ’ГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҘГҳВҜГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВ© ГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷВҒГҷвҖ ГҷЕ ГҳВ© */}
            <Route path="/login" element={<AdminLogin />} />
            <Route path="/admin/dashboard" element={<Dashboard />} />
            <Route path="/admin/tech-dashboard" element={<TechDashboard />} />
            <Route path="/admin/letter-generator" element={<LetterGenerator />} />
          </Routes>
        </div>

        <Partners />
        <Footer />

      </div>
    </Router>
  );
};

export default function App() {
  return (
    <AppProvider>
      <MainApp />
    </AppProvider>
  );
}

                  <p className="text-slate-300 leading-relaxed">{val.desc}</p>
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="py-24 bg-slate-900 text-white relative overflow-hidden" style={{ backgroundImage: "url('https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1565552629477-ff14d7acd490?q=80&w=2070&auto=format&fit=crop')", backgroundSize: "cover", backgroundPosition: "center", backgroundAttachment: "fixed" }}>

          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-4 gap-8">
            {pillars.map((pillar, idx) => {
              const Icon = pillar.icon;
              return (
                <div key={idx} className="text-center p-6 bg-white/5 rounded-3xl border border-white/5 backdrop-blur-sm hover:bg-white/10 transition duration-300">

                    <Icon size={28} />

                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

            <p className="text-slate-500 text-sm leading-relaxed">ГҳВЈГҷвҖ ГҳВёГҷвҖҰГҳВ© ГҷвҖҰГҳВұГҳВ§ГҷвҖҡГҳВЁГҳВ© CCTV ГҷвҖҰГҳВӘГҳВ·ГҷЛҶГҳВұГҳВ©ГҳЕ’ ГҷЛҶГҳВЈГҷвҖҡГҷВҒГҳВ§ГҷвҖһ ГҳВҘГҷвҖһГҷЖ’ГҳВӘГҳВұГҷЛҶГҷвҖ ГҷЕ ГҳВ© ГҳВ°ГҷЖ’ГҷЕ ГҳВ© ГҳВӘГҳВ¶ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖ  ГҷвҖһГҷЖ’ ГҷЛҶГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҳВ§ГҳВҰГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҷЖ’ ГҳВЈГҷвҖҡГҳВөГҷвҖ° ГҳВҜГҳВұГҳВ¬ГҳВ§ГҳВӘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӯГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҷЕ ГҳВ©.</p>
          </div>
          <div className="bg-white p-6 rounded-[2rem] card-hover border border-slate-100 group">

          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

                </div>
                <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/10 backdrop-blur-sm hover:bg-white/10 transition">

                  </div>
                  <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm">ГҳВ№ГҷвҖ  ГҷвҖҰГҳВ·ГҳВ§ГҳВұ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһГҷЖ’ ГҳВ№ГҳВЁГҳВҜГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҳВІГҷЕ ГҳВІ</p>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/10 backdrop-blur-sm hover:bg-white/10 transition">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-2">
                    <Moon className="text-[#c5a059]" size={20} />
                    <span className="font-bold text-lg">ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖҡГҳВ§ГҳВЁГҷвҖһ</span>

                  <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm">ГҷвҖҰГҳВіГҳВ¬ГҳВҜ </p>

                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-2">

                </div>
              </div>

                <iframe title="ГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҷвҖҡГҳВ№ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВҙГҳВұГҷЛҶГҳВ№" width="100%" height="100%" frameBorder="0" style={{ border: 0 }} src="https://maps.google.com/maps?q=Mecca&t=&z=13&ie=UTF8&iwloc=&output=embed" allowFullScreen={true} />
              </div>
              <div className="absolute top-10 -right-4 bg-[#c5a059] p-6 rounded-l-[2rem] shadow-2xl z-20">
                <p className="text-white font-black text-2xl">7</p>
                <p className="text-white/80 font-bold text-sm">ГҷЛҶГҳВӯГҳВҜГҳВ§ГҳВӘ<br />ГҷВҒГҷвҖҡГҳВ·</p>
              </div>
              <a href="https://maps.google.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" className="absolute bottom-8 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 bg-white text-[#1a365d] px-8 py-4 rounded-2xl font-bold shadow-2xl hover:bg-[#c5a059] hover:text-white transition flex items-center gap-3 group z-20 whitespace-nowrap">
                <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-slate-100 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center group-hover:bg-white/20 transition">
                  <MapPin size={20} />
                </div>
                <span>ГҳВ§ГҷВҒГҳВӘГҳВӯ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҷвҖҡГҳВ№ ГҷВҒГҷЕ  ГҳВ®ГҳВұГҳВ§ГҳВҰГҳВ· ГҳВ¬ГҷЛҶГҳВ¬ГҷвҖһ</span>

      <div className="container mx-auto px-6">
        <div className="text-center mb-12">

          <h3 className="text-3xl md:text-4xl font-black text-[#1a365d]">ГҳВ§ГҳВ®ГҳВӘГҳВұ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ·ГҳВ§ГҳВЁГҷвҖҡ ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВіГҳВӘГҳВ№ГҳВұГҳВ§ГҳВ¶ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҳВӯГҳВҜГҳВ§ГҳВӘ</h3>
        </div>
        <div className="flex flex-wrap justify-center gap-4 mb-12">
          {floors.map(f => (
            <button key={f.id} onClick={() => setSelectedFloor(f.id)} className={`px-6 py-3 rounded-full font-bold border-2 border-[#1a365d] transition ${selectedFloor === f.id ? "bg-[#1a365d] text-white" : "text-[#1a365d] hover:bg-[#1a365d]/10"}`}>
              {f.label}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

          <div className="order-2 lg:order-1">
            <h4 className="text-3xl font-black text-[#1a365d] mb-6">ГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҳВөГҷВҒГҳВ§ГҳВӘ {floors.find(f => f.id === selectedFloor).label}</h4>

              <div className="space-y-4">
                <p className="text-slate-500 mb-8 leading-relaxed">ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВӘГҳВ®ГҳВөГҷЕ ГҳВө ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҜГҷЛҶГҳВұ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВЈГҳВұГҳВ¶ГҷЕ  ГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЖ’ГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҷвҖҡГҷВҒ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВіГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҳВұГҳВ§ГҳВӘ ГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ®ГҳВҜГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҳВӘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰГҳВ© ГҷвҖһГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВЁГҷвҖ ГҷвҖ°.</p>
                <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl shadow-sm border border-slate-100 flex items-center gap-4 text-[#1a365d] font-bold">
                  <Car className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҷвҖҡГҷВҒ ГҳВ®ГҳВ§ГҳВөГҳВ©
                </div>
                <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl shadow-sm border border-slate-100 flex items-center gap-4 text-[#1a365d] font-bold">
                  <House className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҷвҖҰГҳВҜГҳВ®ГҷвҖһ ГҷЛҶГҷвҖҰГҳВөГҳВ№ГҳВҜ
                </div>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="space-y-4">
                {unitsData[selectedFloor].map(unit => (
                  <div key={unit.id} className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border border-slate-100 relative overflow-hidden transition-all duration-300 hover:shadow-md">
                    {unit.isSpecial && <div className="absolute top-0 left-0 bg-[#c5a059] text-white text-xs px-3 py-1 rounded-br-lg z-10">ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖҰГҷЕ ГҳВІГҳВ©</div>}
                    {unit.isSold && (
                      <div className="absolute inset-0 z-20 flex items-center justify-center bg-white/50 backdrop-blur-[1px]">
                        <div className="border-[5px] border-red-600 text-red-600 text-3xl font-black px-6 py-2 rounded-xl transform -rotate-12 opacity-80 shadow-lg tracking-wider">ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВЁГҷЕ ГҳВ№ / ГҷвҖҰГҳВӯГҳВ¬ГҷЛҶГҳВІ</div>
                      </div>
                    )}
                    <div className="p-5 cursor-pointer" onClick={() => toggleUnit(unit.id)}>
                      <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                        <div>
                          <span className="block font-bold text-xl text-[#1a365d]">{unit.title}</span>
                          <span className="text-[#c5a059] font-black text-lg">{unit.price}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div className="flex flex-col items-end gap-2 mt-2">
                          <span className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-bold ${unit.isSpecial ? "bg-[#c5a059]/10 text-[#c5a059]" : "bg-slate-100 text-slate-600"}`}>{unit.badge}</span>
                          <ChevronDown className={`text-slate-400 transition-transform duration-300 mt-1 ${expandedUnit === unit.id ? "rotate-180" : ""}`} />
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    {expandedUnit === unit.id && (
                      <div className="px-5 pb-5 bg-slate-50/50 border-t border-slate-100 pt-4 grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 text-sm text-slate-600 animate-fadeIn">
                        <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Ruler size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> {unit.roof ? "422 ГҷвҖҰГӮВІ" : "204 ГҷвҖҰГӮВІ"}</span>
                        <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Bed size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> {unit.roof ? "4 ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒ" : "5 ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒ"}</span>
                        <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><UserCheck size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒГҳВ© ГҳВ®ГҳВ§ГҳВҜГҷвҖҰГҳВ©</span>
                        <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Droplets size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒГҳВ© ГҳВәГҳВіГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ</span>
                        {!unit.roof && <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Fingerprint size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҳВҜГҳВ®ГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ ГҳВ°ГҷЖ’ГҷЕ </span>}
                        {!unit.roof && <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Wifi size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖ ГҳВІГҷвҖһ ГҳВ°ГҷЖ’ГҷЕ </span>}
                        {unit.roof && <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Umbrella size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҳВіГҳВ·ГҳВӯ ГҳВ®ГҳВ§ГҳВө ГҷЖ’ГҳВЁГҷЕ ГҳВұ</span>}
                        {!unit.roof && <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Box size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҷвҖҰГҳВіГҳВӘГҷЛҶГҳВҜГҳВ№</span>}
                        {!unit.roof && <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Car size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҷвҖҡГҷВҒ ГҳВ®ГҳВ§ГҳВө</span>}
                        <span className="col-span-2 flex items-center gap-2"><Layers size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҳВ®ГҳВІГҳВ§ГҷвҖ  ГҳВЈГҳВұГҳВ¶ГҷЕ  ГҷЛҶГҳВ№ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҷЕ  ГҷвҖҰГҳВіГҳВӘГҷвҖҡГҷвҖһ</span>
                        <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Bath size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]" /> 4 ГҳВҜГҷЛҶГҳВұГҳВ§ГҳВӘ ГҷвҖҰГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖЎ</span>
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
          <div className="order-1 lg:order-2 h-full min-h-[400px]">
            <div className="relative group cursor-pointer overflow-hidden rounded-3xl shadow-lg border-4 border-white h-full bg-slate-200 flex items-center justify-center" onClick={() => setPreviewImg(images[selectedFloor])}>
              <div className="absolute top-4 left-4 z-20 w-16 h-16 md:w-24 md:h-24 opacity-50 pointer-events-none mix-blend-multiply">
                <img src={getImg("1I5KIPkeuwJ0CawpWJLpiHdmofSKLQglN")} className="w-full h-full object-contain" alt="Logo" />
              </div>
              <img src={images[selectedFloor]} className="w-full h-full object-cover transform group-hover:scale-105 transition duration-700" alt="ГҷвҖҰГҳВ®ГҳВ·ГҳВ·" />
              <div className="absolute bottom-6 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 bg-white/90 backdrop-blur px-6 py-3 rounded-full text-sm font-bold text-[#1a365d] shadow-lg flex items-center gap-2 transition-transform hover:scale-105">
                <ZoomIn size={16} /> ГҳВ§ГҳВ¶ГҳВәГҳВ· ГҷвҖһГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҷЖ’ГҳВЁГҷЕ ГҳВұ
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const ContactView = ({ showToast }) => {
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setLoading(true);
    
    const payload = {
      name: e.target.name.value,
      phone: e.target.phone.value,
      unit: e.target.unit.value,
    };

    try {
      const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}?action=add_lead`, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(payload)
      });
      if (response.ok) {
        showToast("ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҘГҳВұГҳВіГҳВ§ГҷвҖһ ГҳВЁГҷвҖ ГҳВ¬ГҳВ§ГҳВӯ", "ГҳВҙГҷЖ’ГҳВұГҳВ§ГҷвҖ№ ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҷвҖЎГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰГҷЖ’ГҳЕ’ ГҳВіГҷЕ ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҳВөГҷвҖһ ГҷвҖҰГҳВ№ГҷЖ’ ГҷвҖҡГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҷвҖ№.");
        e.target.reset();
      } else {
        throw new Error("ГҷВҒГҳВҙГҷвҖһ");
      }
    } catch {
      showToast("ГҳВӘГҷвҖ ГҳВЁГҷЕ ГҷвҖЎ", "ГҳВӯГҳВҜГҳВ« ГҳВ®ГҳВ·ГҳВЈ ГҷВҒГҷЕ  ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВӘГҳВөГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳЕ’ ГҷЕ ГҳВұГҳВ¬ГҷвҖ° ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВӯГҳВ§ГҷЛҶГҷвҖһГҳВ© ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВӯГҷвҖҡГҳВ§ГҷвҖ№.", "error");
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="pt-32 pb-20 min-h-screen relative flex items-center bg-cover bg-center" style={{ backgroundImage: `url('${getImg("18fCsrolSEvo8q9wt2_z4BXlB88BZ-62-")}')` }}>
      <div className="absolute inset-0 hero-gradient" />
      <div className="container mx-auto px-6 relative z-10 max-w-5xl">
        <div className="bg-slate-900/60 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-[3rem] shadow-2xl overflow-hidden flex flex-col lg:flex-row border border-white/10">
          <div className="lg:w-1/2 p-12 md:p-20 flex flex-col justify-center text-white">
            <h2 className="text-4xl font-black mb-6">ГҳВ§ГҳВӯГҳВ¬ГҳВІ ГҷЛҶГҳВӯГҳВҜГҳВӘГҷЖ’ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВіГҷЖ’ГҷвҖ ГҷЕ ГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВўГҷвҖ </h2>
            <p className="text-slate-200 text-lg mb-10 leading-relaxed">ГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҳВҜГҳВұ ГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВіГҳВ¬ГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһГҷЖ’ ГҷЛҶГҳВӯГҳВҜГҳВӘГҷЖ’ ГҷВҒГҷЕ  ГҷвҖЎГҳВ°ГҳВ§ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВҙГҳВұГҷЛҶГҳВ№.</p>
            <div className="space-y-4 mb-10">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-xl font-bold">
                <Phone className="text-[#c5a059]" /> 920032842
              </div>
              <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-xl font-bold">
                <MapPin className="text-[#c5a059]" /> ГҳВӯГҷЕ  ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВЁГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҳВЁГҳВ©ГҳЕ’ ГҷвҖҰГҷЖ’ГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЖ’ГҳВұГҷвҖҰГҳВ©
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="lg:w-1/2 bg-slate-900/30 p-12 md:p-20 border-r border-white/10">
            <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-6">
              <div>
                <label className="block text-sm font-bold mb-2 text-slate-200">ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВіГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЖ’ГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ</label>
                <input type="text" name="name" required className="w-full bg-white/10 border border-white/20 px-6 py-4 rounded-2xl outline-none focus:border-[#c5a059] text-white placeholder-gray-400 transition" placeholder="ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВіГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ«ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВ«ГҷЕ " />
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="block text-sm font-bold mb-2 text-slate-200">ГҳВұГҷвҖҡГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ¬ГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҷвҖһ</label>
                <input type="tel" name="phone" required className="w-full bg-white/10 border border-white/20 px-6 py-4 rounded-2xl outline-none focus:border-[#c5a059] text-white placeholder-gray-400 transition" placeholder="05xxxxxxxx" />
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="block text-sm font-bold mb-2 text-slate-200">ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҳВӯГҳВҜГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷвҖЎГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВЁГҷвҖЎГҳВ§</label>
                <select name="unit" className="w-full bg-white/10 border border-white/20 px-6 py-4 rounded-2xl outline-none focus:border-[#c5a059] text-white transition [&>option]:text-slate-900" defaultValue="">
                  <option value="" disabled>ГҳВ§ГҳВ®ГҳВӘГҳВұ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҳВӯГҳВҜГҳВ©</option>
                  <option value="SM-A01">SM-A01</option>
                  <option value="SM-A02">SM-A02</option>
                  <option value="SM-A03">SM-A03</option>
                  <option value="SM-A04">SM-A04</option>
                  <option value="SM-A05" disabled className="text-red-500 bg-red-100">SM-A05 (ГҷвҖҰГҳВӯГҳВ¬ГҷЛҶГҳВІГҳВ©)</option>
                  <option value="SM-A06">SM-A06</option>
                  <option value="SM-A07" disabled className="text-red-500 bg-red-100">SM-A07 (ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВЁГҷЕ ГҳВ№)</option>
                </select>
              </div>
              <button type="submit" disabled={loading} className="w-full bg-[#c5a059] text-white py-5 rounded-2xl font-black text-xl hover:bg-yellow-600 transition flex justify-center items-center gap-2 shadow-xl">
                {loading ? <RefreshCw className="animate-spin" /> : <Send />} ГҳВҘГҳВұГҳВіГҳВ§ГҷвҖһ ГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҷвҖЎГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰ
              </button>
            </form>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const AdminLoginView = ({ setUser, navigateTo, showToast }) => {
  const [email, setEmail] = useState("");
  const [password, setPassword] = useState("");
  const [rememberMe, setRememberMe] = useState(false);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    const savedEmail = localStorage.getItem("semak_admin_email");
    const savedPassword = localStorage.getItem("semak_admin_password");
    if (savedEmail && savedPassword) {
      setEmail(savedEmail);
      setPassword(savedPassword);
      setRememberMe(true);
    }
  }, []);

  const handleLogin = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}?action=login`, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ email, password })
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      
      if (data.success) {
        if (rememberMe) {
          localStorage.setItem("semak_admin_email", email);
          localStorage.setItem("semak_admin_password", password);
        } else {
          localStorage.removeItem("semak_admin_email");
          localStorage.removeItem("semak_admin_password");
        }
        setUser(data.user);
        showToast("ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВӘГҳВіГҳВ¬ГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҜГҳВ®ГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ", `ГҷвҖҰГҳВұГҳВӯГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҷвҖ№ ГҳВЁГҷЖ’ГҳЕ’ ${data.user.name}`);
        
        if (data.user.role === "technician") {
          navigateTo("tech-dashboard");
        } else {
          navigateTo("dashboard");
        }
      } else {
        showToast("ГҳВ®ГҳВ·ГҳВЈ", data.message, "error");
      }
    } catch {
      showToast("ГҳВ®ГҳВ·ГҳВЈ", "ГҷВҒГҳВҙГҷвҖһ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВӘГҳВөГҳВ§ГҷвҖһ ГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВіГҷЕ ГҳВұГҷВҒГҳВұ", "error");
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-cover bg-center relative" style={{ backgroundImage: "url('https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1497366216548-37526070297c?q=80&w=2069&auto=format&fit=crop')" }}>
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[#1a365d]/90 backdrop-blur-sm" />
      <div className="bg-white p-10 md:p-12 rounded-[2.5rem] shadow-2xl max-w-md w-full text-center relative z-10 border border-white/20">
        <img src={getImg("1I5KIPkeuwJ0CawpWJLpiHdmofSKLQglN")} alt="ГҳВіГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҷЖ’ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҡГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВ©" className="h-16 mx-auto mb-4 object-contain" />
        <h2 className="text-2xl font-black text-[#1a365d]">ГҳВЁГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҳВЁГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҳВёГҷВҒГҷЕ ГҷвҖ </h2>
        <p className="text-slate-500 text-sm mt-2 mb-8">ГҳВӘГҳВіГҳВ¬ГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҜГҳВ®ГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ ГҷвҖһГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҳВөГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ ГҷвҖһГҷвҖһГҳВЈГҳВҜГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҳВӘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҘГҳВҜГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВ© ГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷВҒГҷвҖ ГҷЕ ГҳВ©</p>
        <form onSubmit={handleLogin} className="space-y-6 text-right">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-bold mb-2 text-[#1a365d]">ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВЁГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВҜ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҘГҷвҖһГҷЖ’ГҳВӘГҳВұГҷЛҶГҷвҖ ГҷЕ </label>
            <div className="relative">
              <span className="absolute right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-slate-400"><User size={16} /></span>
              <input type="email" value={email} onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)} required className="w-full bg-slate-50 border border-slate-200 px-6 py-4 pr-12 rounded-xl outline-none focus:border-[#c5a059] focus:bg-white text-slate-800 transition" placeholder="Email" />
            </div>
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-bold mb-2 text-[#1a365d]">ГҷЖ’ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВұГҷЛҶГҳВұ</label>
            <div className="relative">
              <span className="absolute right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-slate-400"><Lock size={16} /></span>
              <input type="password" value={password} onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)} required className="w-full bg-slate-50 border border-slate-200 px-6 py-4 pr-12 rounded-xl outline-none focus:border-[#c5a059] focus:bg-white text-slate-800 transition" placeholder="ГўвӮ¬ВўГўвӮ¬ВўГўвӮ¬ВўГўвӮ¬ВўГўвӮ¬ВўГўвӮ¬ВўГўвӮ¬ВўГўвӮ¬Вў" />
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-2">
            <input type="checkbox" id="rememberMe" checked={rememberMe} onChange={(e) => setRememberMe(e.target.checked)} className="w-4 h-4 accent-[#c5a059] cursor-pointer rounded border-slate-300"/>
            <label htmlFor="rememberMe" className="text-sm text-slate-600 font-bold cursor-pointer select-none">ГҳВӘГҳВ°ГҷЖ’ГҳВұ ГҳВЁГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖ ГҳВ§ГҳВӘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҜГҳВ®ГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ</label>
          </div>
          <button type="submit" disabled={loading} className="w-full bg-[#1a365d] text-white py-4 rounded-xl font-bold text-lg hover:bg-[#c5a059] transition shadow-lg shadow-[#1a365d]/30 mt-4 flex justify-center items-center gap-2">
            {loading ? <RefreshCw className="animate-spin" size={20} /> : "ГҳВҜГҳВ®ГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ"}
          </button>
        </form>
        <div className="mt-8 text-center pt-6 border-t border-slate-100">
          <button onClick={() => navigateTo("home")} className="text-slate-400 hover:text-[#1a365d] text-sm flex items-center justify-center gap-2 mx-auto transition">
            <ArrowRight size={14} /> ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷЛҶГҳВҜГҳВ© ГҷвҖһГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҷвҖҡГҳВ№ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВұГҳВҰГҷЕ ГҳВіГҷЕ 
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const CustomerLoginView = ({ setCustomer, navigateTo, showToast }) => {
  const handleLogin = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const user = e.target.user.value;
    const pass = e.target.password.value;
    if (user === "user" && pass === "user") {
      setCustomer({ username: "user", name: "ГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ ГҳВӘГҳВ¬ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВЁГҷЕ ", unit: "SM-A01" });
      showToast("ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВӘГҳВіГҳВ¬ГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҜГҳВ®ГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ ГҳВЁГҷвҖ ГҳВ¬ГҳВ§ГҳВӯ", "ГҷвҖҰГҳВұГҳВӯГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҷвҖ№ ГҳВЁГҷЖ’ ГҷВҒГҷЕ  ГҳВЁГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҳВЁГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВЎ");
      navigateTo("maintenance");
    } else {
      showToast("ГҳВ®ГҳВ·ГҳВЈ", "ГҳВЁГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖ ГҳВ§ГҳВӘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҜГҳВ®ГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ ГҳВәГҷЕ ГҳВұ ГҳВөГҳВӯГҷЕ ГҳВӯГҳВ©", "error");
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-cover bg-center relative" style={{ backgroundImage: "url('https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1560518883-ce09059eeffa?q=80&w=2073&auto=format&fit=crop')" }}>
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[#1a365d]/90 backdrop-blur-sm" />
      <div className="bg-white p-10 md:p-12 rounded-[2.5rem] shadow-2xl max-w-md w-full text-center relative z-10 border border-white/20">
        <div className="w-16 h-16 bg-[#c5a059]/10 text-[#c5a059] rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center text-3xl mx-auto mb-4">
          <ShieldCheck size={32} />
        </div>
        <h2 className="text-2xl font-black text-[#1a365d]">ГҳВЁГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҳВЁГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВЎ</h2>
        <p className="text-slate-500 text-sm mt-2 mb-8">ГҳВӘГҳВіГҳВ¬ГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҜГҳВ®ГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ ГҷвҖһГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁ ГҷЛҶ ГҷвҖҰГҳВӘГҳВ§ГҳВЁГҳВ№ГҳВ© ГҳВ®ГҳВҜГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҳВӘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВөГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖ ГҳВ©</p>
        <form onSubmit={handleLogin} className="space-y-6 text-right">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-bold mb-2 text-[#1a365d]">ГҳВ§ГҳВіГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВіГҳВӘГҳВ®ГҳВҜГҷвҖҰ</label>
            <div className="relative">
              <span className="absolute right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-slate-400"><User size={16} /></span>
              <input type="text" name="user" required className="w-full bg-slate-50 border border-slate-200 px-6 py-4 pr-12 rounded-xl outline-none focus:border-[#c5a059] focus:bg-white text-slate-800 transition" placeholder="user" />
            </div>
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-bold mb-2 text-[#1a365d]">ГҷЖ’ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВұГҷЛҶГҳВұ</label>
            <div className="relative">
              <span className="absolute right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-slate-400"><Lock size={16} /></span>
              <input type="password" name="password" required className="w-full bg-slate-50 border border-slate-200 px-6 py-4 pr-12 rounded-xl outline-none focus:border-[#c5a059] focus:bg-white text-slate-800 transition" placeholder="user" />
            </div>
          </div>
          <button type="submit" className="w-full bg-[#c5a059] text-white py-4 rounded-xl font-bold text-lg hover:bg-yellow-600 transition shadow-lg shadow-[#c5a059]/30 mt-4">ГҳВҜГҳВ®ГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ</button>
        </form>
        <div className="mt-6 p-4 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl text-xs text-slate-500 text-center">
          <strong>ГҳВӯГҳВіГҳВ§ГҳВЁ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВ¬ГҳВұГҳВЁГҳВ©:</strong> (user / user)
        </div>
        <div className="mt-8 text-center pt-6 border-t border-slate-100">
          <button onClick={() => navigateTo("home")} className="text-slate-400 hover:text-[#1a365d] text-sm flex items-center justify-center gap-2 mx-auto transition">
            <ArrowRight size={14} /> ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷЛҶГҳВҜГҳВ© ГҷвҖһГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҷвҖҡГҳВ№ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВұГҳВҰГҷЕ ГҳВіГҷЕ 
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const MaintenanceView = ({ customer, setCustomer, navigateTo, showToast }) => {
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [tab, setTab] = useState("new");
  const [type, setType] = useState("");
  const [date, setDate] = useState("");
  const [time, setTime] = useState("");
  const [ticket, setTicket] = useState(null);

  const handleLogout = () => {
    setCustomer(null);
    showToast("ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВӘГҳВіГҳВ¬ГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ®ГҳВұГҷЛҶГҳВ¬", "ГҷвҖ ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҷвҖ ГҷвҖ° ГҷвҖһГҷЖ’ ГҷЕ ГҷЛҶГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҷвҖ№ ГҳВіГҳВ№ГҷЕ ГҳВҜГҳВ§ГҷвҖ№");
    navigateTo("home");
  };

  const submitTicket = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!date || !time) {
      showToast("ГҳВӘГҷвҖ ГҳВЁГҷЕ ГҷвҖЎ", "ГҷЕ ГҳВұГҳВ¬ГҷвҖ° ГҳВ§ГҳВ®ГҳВӘГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҳВұ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВ® ГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҷвҖҡГҳВӘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷвҖ ГҳВ§ГҳВіГҳВЁ ГҷвҖһГҳВІГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҳВұГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷВҒГҷвҖ ГҷЕ ", "error");
      return;
    }
    setLoading(true);
    
    const desc = `ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҷвҖҡГҳВӘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷВҒГҳВ¶ГҷвҖһ: ${time}\nГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВ® ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷВҒГҳВ¶ГҷвҖһ: ${date}\n\nГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҳВөГҷВҒ:\n${e.target.desc.value}`;
    
    const payload = {
      name: e.target.name.value,
      phone: e.target.phone.value,
      unit: e.target.unit.value,
      type: e.target.type.value,
      desc: desc
    };

    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}?action=add_maintenance`, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(payload)
      });
      const result = await res.json();
      
      showToast("ГҷвҖ ГҳВ¬ГҳВ§ГҳВӯ", "ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҳВіГҳВӘГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁГҷЖ’ ГҷЛҶГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҷвҖ ГҳВӘГҳВёГҳВ§ГҳВұ ГҳВ§ГҳВ№ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҳВҜ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҳВ№ГҳВҜ ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖ  ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҘГҳВҜГҳВ§ГҳВұГҳВ©.");
      e.target.reset();
      setDate("");
      setTime("");
      setTicket({...payload, id: result.id, status: "ГҷвҖҡГҷЕ ГҳВҜ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҷвҖ ГҳВӘГҳВёГҳВ§ГҳВұ", technician: "ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰ ГҷЕ ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВ№ГҷЕ ГҷЕ ГҷвҖ ", scheduleDate: date, scheduleTime: time});
      setTab("track");
    } catch {
      showToast("ГҳВӘГҷвҖ ГҳВЁГҷЕ ГҷвҖЎ", "ГҳВӯГҳВҜГҳВ« ГҳВ®ГҳВ·ГҳВЈ. ГҳВӯГҳВ§ГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВӯГҷвҖҡГҳВ§ГҷвҖ№.", "error");
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const renderTracker = () => {
    if (!ticket) return <div className="text-center py-10 text-slate-500">ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ ГҷЕ ГҷЛҶГҳВ¬ГҳВҜ ГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҳВӘ ГҳВіГҳВ§ГҳВЁГҷвҖҡГҳВ©.</div>;
    
    const steps = [
      { id: 1, label: "ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҳВіГҳВӘГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁ", status: "ГҷвҖҡГҷЕ ГҳВҜ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҷвҖ ГҳВӘГҳВёГҳВ§ГҳВұ", icon: ListChecks, desc: "ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҳВіГҳВӘГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁГҷЖ’ ГҷЛҶГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҷвҖ ГҳВӘГҳВёГҳВ§ГҳВұ ГҷвҖҰГҳВұГҳВ§ГҳВ¬ГҳВ№ГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ¬ГҳВҜГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ." },
      { id: 2, label: "ГҳВӘГҳВЈГҷЖ’ГҷЕ ГҳВҜ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҳВ№ГҳВҜ ГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷВҒГҷвҖ ГҷЕ ", status: "ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҳВ№ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҳВҜ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҳВ№ГҳВҜ", icon: CalendarDays, desc: `ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВ№ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҳВҜ. ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷВҒГҷвҖ ГҷЕ : ${ticket.technician && ticket.technician !== "ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰ ГҷЕ ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВ№ГҷЕ ГҷЕ ГҷвҖ " ? ticket.technician : "ГҳВіГҷЕ ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВӯГҳВҜГҷЕ ГҳВҜ"} | ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҳВ№ГҳВҜ: ${ticket.scheduleDate || "ГҳВіГҷЕ ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВЈГҷЖ’ГҷЕ ГҳВҜ"} (${ticket.scheduleTime || ""})` },
      { id: 3, label: "ГҳВ¬ГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ  ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ", status: "ГҳВ¬ГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ  ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ", icon: HardHat, desc: "ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷВҒГҷвҖ ГҷЕ  ГҷВҒГҷЕ  ГҳВ·ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҷвҖҡГҷвҖЎ ГҳВҘГҷвҖһГҷЕ ГҷЖ’ ГҳВЈГҷЛҶ ГҷЕ ГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҳВҙГҳВұ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ ГҳВӯГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖ№." },
      { id: 4, label: "ГҷвҖҰГҷЖ’ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ", status: "ГҷвҖҰГҷЖ’ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ", icon: CircleCheck, desc: "ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВҘГҳВәГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҷвҖҡ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁГҳЕ’ ГҳВҙГҷЖ’ГҳВұГҳВ§ГҷвҖ№ ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВ№ГҳВ§ГҷЛҶГҷвҖ ГҷЖ’ГҷвҖҰ." }
    ];
    
    let currentStep = 0;
    if (["ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВ№ГҷЕ ГҷЕ ГҷвҖ ", "ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҳВ№ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҳВҜ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҳВ№ГҳВҜ", "ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖҡГҳВӘГҳВұГҳВ§ГҳВӯ ГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҳВ№ГҳВҜ ГҳВЁГҳВҜГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ"].includes(ticket.status)) currentStep = 1;
    if (ticket.status === "ГҳВ¬ГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ  ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ") currentStep = 2;
    if (ticket.status === "ГҷвҖҰГҷЖ’ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ") currentStep = 3;

    return (
      <div className="bg-white p-8 md:p-10 rounded-[2.5rem] shadow-2xl border border-slate-100 relative overflow-hidden animate-fade-in-up">
        <div className="absolute top-0 right-0 w-full h-2 bg-[#1a365d]" />
        <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-10 border-b border-slate-100 pb-6">
          <div>
            <h4 className="text-2xl font-black text-[#1a365d] mb-2">ГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁ ГҳВұГҷвҖҡГҷвҖҰ {ticket.id}</h4>
            <p className="text-slate-500 flex items-center gap-2"><Clock size={16} /> ГҳВӘГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВ® ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁ: {ticket.date || new Date().toLocaleDateString("ar-EG")}</p>
          </div>
          <span className="bg-[#c5a059]/10 text-[#c5a059] px-4 py-2 rounded-xl font-bold text-sm border border-[#c5a059]/20">{ticket.type}</span>
        </div>
        <div className="timeline-container pr-4">
          {steps.map((step, i) => {
            const Icon = step.icon;
            const isPast = i <= currentStep;
            const isCurrent = i === currentStep;
            return (
              <div key={step.id} className="timeline-item">
                <div className={`timeline-icon ${isPast ? "bg-[#c5a059] text-white shadow-lg shadow-orange-200" : "bg-slate-200 text-slate-400"}`}>
                  <Icon size={16} />
                </div>
                <div className={`bg-slate-50 rounded-2xl p-5 border ${isCurrent ? "border-[#c5a059] shadow-md" : "border-slate-100"} transition-all`}>
                  <h5 className={`font-bold text-lg mb-1 ${isCurrent ? "text-[#c5a059]" : "text-[#1a365d]"}`}>{step.label}</h5>
                  <p className="text-slate-500 text-sm">{step.desc}</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  return (
    <div className="pt-32 pb-20 bg-slate-50 min-h-screen relative flex items-center justify-center bg-cover bg-center" style={{ backgroundImage: "url('https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1581094794329-c8112a89af12?q=80&w=2070&auto=format&fit=crop')" }}>
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[#1a365d]/90 backdrop-blur-sm" />
      <div className="w-full max-w-3xl px-6 relative z-10">
        <div className="text-center mb-10 text-white relative">
          <button onClick={handleLogout} className="absolute left-0 top-0 bg-red-500/20 text-red-100 hover:bg-red-500 hover:text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-xl transition text-sm font-bold flex items-center gap-2 backdrop-blur-md border border-red-500/30">
            <LogOut size={16} /> ГҳВ®ГҳВұГҷЛҶГҳВ¬
          </button>
          <h2 className="text-[#c5a059] font-black tracking-[0.1em] uppercase text-sm mb-2">ГҳВЁГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҳВЁГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВЎ</h2>
          <h3 className="text-3xl md:text-4xl font-black mb-6">ГҳВҘГҳВҜГҳВ§ГҳВұГҳВ© ГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҳВӘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВөГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖ ГҳВ©</h3>
          <div className="flex justify-center gap-4 bg-white/10 p-2 rounded-full backdrop-blur-md w-fit mx-auto border border-white/10">
            <button onClick={() => setTab("new")} className={`px-6 py-2 rounded-full font-bold text-sm transition ${tab === "new" ? "bg-[#c5a059] text-white shadow-lg" : "text-slate-300 hover:text-white"}`}>ГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁ ГҳВ¬ГҳВҜГҷЕ ГҳВҜ</button>
            <button onClick={() => setTab("track")} className={`px-6 py-2 rounded-full font-bold text-sm transition ${tab === "track" ? "bg-[#c5a059] text-white shadow-lg" : "text-slate-300 hover:text-white"}`}>ГҷвҖҰГҳВӘГҳВ§ГҳВЁГҳВ№ГҳВ© ГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҳВӘГҷЕ </button>
          </div>
        </div>
        {tab === "new" ? (
          <div className="bg-white p-8 md:p-10 rounded-[2.5rem] shadow-2xl border border-slate-100 relative overflow-hidden animate-fade-in-up">
            <div className="absolute top-0 right-0 w-full h-2 bg-gradient-to-r from-[#c5a059] to-yellow-600" />
            <form onSubmit={submitTicket} className="space-y-6">
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-sm font-bold mb-2 text-[#1a365d]">ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВіГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЖ’ГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ</label>
                  <input type="text" name="name" defaultValue={customer?.name} required className="w-full bg-slate-50 border border-slate-200 px-5 py-3 rounded-2xl outline-none focus:border-[#c5a059] transition shadow-sm" placeholder="ГҳВ§ГҳВіГҷвҖҰГҷЖ’ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЖ’ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҷвҖҰ" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-sm font-bold mb-2 text-[#1a365d]">ГҳВұГҷвҖҡГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ¬ГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҷвҖһ</label>
                  <input type="tel" name="phone" required className="w-full bg-slate-50 border border-slate-200 px-5 py-3 rounded-2xl outline-none focus:border-[#c5a059] transition shadow-sm" placeholder="05xxxxxxxx" />
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-sm font-bold mb-2 text-[#1a365d]">ГҳВұГҷвҖҡГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҳВӯГҳВҜГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҡГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВ©</label>
                  <input type="text" name="unit" defaultValue={customer?.unit} readOnly={!!customer?.unit} required className={`w-full bg-slate-50 border border-slate-200 px-5 py-3 rounded-2xl outline-none transition shadow-sm ${customer?.unit ? "bg-slate-100 cursor-not-allowed text-slate-500" : "focus:border-[#c5a059]"}`} placeholder="ГҷвҖҰГҳВ«ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһ: SM-A01" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-sm font-bold mb-2 text-[#1a365d]">ГҷвҖ ГҷЛҶГҳВ№ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҳВ·ГҷвҖһ</label>
                  <select name="type" required value={type} onChange={e => setType(e.target.value)} className="w-full bg-slate-50 border border-slate-200 px-5 py-3 rounded-2xl outline-none focus:border-[#c5a059] transition shadow-sm">
                    <option value="" disabled>ГҳВ§ГҳВ®ГҳВӘГҳВұ ГҷвҖ ГҷЛҶГҳВ№ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҳВ·ГҷвҖһ...</option>
                    <option value="ГҳВӘГҷЖ’ГҷЕ ГҷЕ ГҷВҒ">ГҳВӘГҷЖ’ГҷЕ ГҷЕ ГҷВҒ</option>
                    <option value="ГҳВіГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҷЖ’ГҳВ©">ГҳВіГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҷЖ’ГҳВ©</option>
                    <option value="ГҷЖ’ГҷвҖЎГҳВұГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҳВЎ">ГҷЖ’ГҷвҖЎГҳВұГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҳВЎ</option>
                    <option value="ГҳВЈГҳВ®ГҳВұГҷвҖ°">ГҳВЈГҳВ®ГҳВұГҷвҖ°</option>
                  </select>
                </div>
              </div>
              {type && (
                <div className="bg-blue-50/50 p-6 rounded-2xl border border-blue-100 animate-fadeIn">
                  <h4 className="text-sm font-bold text-blue-800 mb-4 flex items-center gap-2"><CalendarDays size={16} /> ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҳВ№ГҳВҜ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷВҒГҳВ¶ГҷвҖһ ГҷвҖһГҷвҖһГҳВІГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҳВұГҳВ© (ГҳВӯГҳВіГҳВЁ ГҳВ¬ГҳВҜГҷЛҶГҷвҖһ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷВҒГҷвҖ ГҷЕ )</h4>
                  <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
                    <div>
                      <label className="block text-xs font-bold mb-2 text-slate-500">ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВ® ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷвҖ ГҳВ§ГҳВіГҳВЁ ГҷвҖһГҷЖ’</label>
                      <input type="date" min={new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0]} required value={date} onChange={e => setDate(e.target.value)} className="w-full bg-white border border-blue-200 px-4 py-3 rounded-xl outline-none focus:border-blue-500 transition shadow-sm text-sm" />
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <label className="block text-xs font-bold mb-2 text-slate-500">ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҷвҖҡГҳВӘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВӘГҳВ§ГҳВӯ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷВҒГҳВ¶ГҷвҖһ</label>
                      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
                        {TIME_SLOTS.map(t => (
                          <div key={t} onClick={() => setTime(t)} className={`text-xs font-bold text-center py-3 rounded-xl cursor-pointer transition-all border ${time === t ? "bg-blue-600 text-white border-blue-600 shadow-md transform scale-105" : "bg-white text-slate-600 border-blue-100 hover:border-blue-300"}`}>
                            {t}
                          </div>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  {date && time && (
                    <div className="mt-4 text-xs text-blue-600 font-bold bg-blue-100 p-3 rounded-lg flex justify-between items-center">
                      <span>ГҳВіГҷвҖ ГҷвҖҡГҷЛҶГҷвҖҰ ГҳВЁГҷвҖҰГҳВұГҳВ§ГҳВ¬ГҳВ№ГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҳВ№ГҳВҜ ГҷЛҶГҳВӘГҳВЈГҷЖ’ГҷЕ ГҳВҜГҷвҖЎ ГҷвҖҰГҳВ№ГҷЖ’.</span>
                      <span>ГҳВӘГҷВҒГҳВ¶ГҷЕ ГҷвҖһГҷЖ’: {date} | {time}</span>
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              )}
              <div>
                <label className="block text-sm font-bold mb-2 text-[#1a365d]">ГҷЛҶГҳВөГҷВҒ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВҙГҷЖ’ГҷвҖһГҳВ© ГҳВЁГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҷВҒГҳВөГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ</label>
                <textarea name="desc" rows="3" required className="w-full bg-slate-50 border border-slate-200 px-5 py-3 rounded-2xl outline-none focus:border-[#c5a059] transition shadow-sm" placeholder="ГҷЕ ГҳВұГҳВ¬ГҷвҖ° ГҷЛҶГҳВөГҷВҒ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҳВ·ГҷвҖһ ГҷвҖЎГҷвҖ ГҳВ§..." />
              </div>
              <button type="submit" disabled={loading} className="w-full bg-[#c5a059] text-white px-8 py-4 rounded-full font-bold hover:bg-yellow-600 transition shadow-lg shadow-[#c5a059]/20 transform hover:-translate-y-1 text-lg flex justify-center items-center gap-2">
                {loading ? <RefreshCw className="animate-spin" /> : <Send />} ГҳВҘГҳВұГҳВіГҳВ§ГҷвҖһ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁ
              </button>
            </form>
          </div>
        ) : renderTracker()}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

// --- ГҳВЁГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҳВЁГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷВҒГҷвҖ ГҷЕ ГҷЕ ГҷвҖ  ---
const TechDashboardView = ({ user, setUser, navigateTo, showToast }) => {
  const [tickets, setTickets] = useState([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [otpInputs, setOtpInputs] = useState({});

  const handleLogout = () => {
    setUser(null);
    navigateTo("home");
  };

  const loadMyTickets = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}?action=get_maintenance`);
      let data = await res.json();
      
      const myTickets = data.filter(t => t.technician === user.name).map(row => {
         let desc = row.descrip || "---";
         let scheduleDate = row.date ? row.date.split(" ")[0] : "";
         let scheduleTime = "ГҳВәГҷЕ ГҳВұ ГҷвҖҰГҳВӯГҳВҜГҳВҜ";
         if (desc.includes("ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВ® ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷВҒГҳВ¶ГҷвҖһ:")) {
           const dateMatch = desc.match(/ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ ГҳВ® ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷВҒГҳВ¶ГҷвҖһ: (.*)/);
           if (dateMatch) scheduleDate = dateMatch[1];
           const timeMatch = desc.match(/ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҷвҖҡГҳВӘ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷВҒГҳВ¶ГҷвҖһ: (.*)/);
           if (timeMatch) scheduleTime = timeMatch[1];
           desc = desc.split(`\n\nГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҳВөГҷВҒ:\n`)[1] || desc;
         }
         return { ...row, scheduleDate, scheduleTime, desc };
      });
      setTickets(myTickets);
    } catch (err) {
      showToast("ГҳВ®ГҳВ·ГҳВЈ", "ГҳВӘГҳВ№ГҳВ°ГҳВұ ГҳВ¬ГҷвҖһГҳВЁ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷвҖЎГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰ", "error");
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => { loadMyTickets(); }, []);

  const updateStatus = async (id, newStatus) => {
    setTickets(prev => prev.map(t => t.id === id ? { ...t, status: newStatus } : t));
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}?action=update_maintenance`, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ ticket_id: id, field_name: "status", new_value: newStatus })
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (data.success) {
        showToast("ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВӯГҳВҜГҷЕ ГҳВ«", `ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВӘГҳВӯГҳВҜГҷЕ ГҳВ« ГҳВӯГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ·ГҷвҖһГҳВЁ ГҳВҘГҷвҖһГҷвҖ°: ${newStatus}`);
      }
    } catch (error) { showToast("ГҳВ®ГҳВ·ГҳВЈ", "ГҳВӘГҳВ№ГҳВ°ГҳВұ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҳВӘГҳВөГҳВ§ГҷвҖһ ГҳВЁГҷвҖҡГҳВ§ГҳВ№ГҳВҜГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВЁГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖ ГҳВ§ГҳВӘ.", "error"); }
  };

  const handleOtpSubmit = (ticket) => {
    const enteredOtp = otpInputs[ticket.id];
    if (enteredOtp === ticket.otp) {
      updateStatus(ticket.id, "ГҷвҖҰГҷЖ’ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ");
    } else {
      showToast("ГҳВұГҷвҖҰГҳВІ ГҳВ®ГҳВ§ГҳВ·ГҳВҰ", "ГҳВұГҷвҖҰГҳВІ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҷВҒГҳВ№ГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ (OTP) ГҳВәГҷЕ ГҳВұ ГҳВөГҳВӯГҷЕ ГҳВӯГҳЕ’ ГҷЕ ГҳВұГҳВ¬ГҷвҖ° ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВЈГҷЖ’ГҳВҜ ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖ  ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ.", "error");
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="pt-24 pb-20 bg-slate-50 min-h-screen">
      <div className="container mx-auto px-4 max-w-3xl">
        <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-8 bg-white p-6 rounded-[2rem] shadow-sm border border-slate-100">
          <div>
            <h1 className="text-2xl font-black text-[#1a365d]">ГҳВЁГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҳВЁГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷвҖЎГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰ</h1>
            <p className="text-slate-500 text-sm mt-1">ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷВҒГҷвҖ ГҷЕ : <span className="font-bold text-[#c5a059]">{user?.name}</span></p>
          </div>
          <button onClick={handleLogout} className="bg-red-50 text-red-600 p-3 rounded-xl hover:bg-red-600 hover:text-white transition">
            <LogOut size={20} />
          </button>
        </div>

        {loading ? (
          <div className="text-center py-20 text-[#c5a059]"><RefreshCw className="animate-spin inline mr-2" /> ГҳВ¬ГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ  ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВӘГҳВӯГҷвҖҰГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ...</div>
        ) : tickets.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="text-center py-20 bg-white rounded-3xl border border-slate-100"><p className="text-slate-500">ГҷвҖһГҳВ§ ГҳВӘГҷЛҶГҳВ¬ГҳВҜ ГҷвҖһГҳВҜГҷЕ ГҷЖ’ ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖЎГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰ ГҷвҖҰГҳВіГҷвҖ ГҳВҜГҳВ© ГҳВӯГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖ№.</p></div>
        ) : (
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {tickets.map(ticket => (
              <div key={ticket.id} className="bg-white p-6 rounded-3xl shadow-sm border border-slate-200">
                <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-4">
                  <div className="flex gap-2">
                    <span className="bg-purple-100 text-purple-700 px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-xs font-black">#{ticket.id}</span>
                    <span className="bg-slate-100 text-slate-700 px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold">{ticket.type}</span>
                  </div>
                  <span className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold ${ticket.status === 'ГҷвҖҰГҷЖ’ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ' ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' : ticket.status === 'ГҳВ¬ГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ  ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ' ? 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-700' : 'bg-orange-100 text-orange-700'}`}>
                    {ticket.status}
                  </span>
                </div>
                
                <h3 className="font-black text-lg text-[#1a365d] mb-2">{ticket.unit}</h3>
                <div className="bg-slate-50 p-4 rounded-xl text-sm text-slate-600 mb-4 border border-slate-100">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2 font-bold text-[#1a365d]"><CalendarDays size={16} className="text-[#c5a059]"/> {ticket.scheduleDate} | {ticket.scheduleTime}</div>
                  <p className="border-t border-slate-200 pt-2 mt-2 leading-relaxed">{ticket.desc}</p>
                </div>

                {ticket.status === "ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҳВ№ГҳВӘГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҳВҜ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҳВ№ГҳВҜ" && (
                  <button onClick={() => updateStatus(ticket.id, "ГҳВ¬ГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ  ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ")} className="w-full bg-[#1a365d] text-white py-3 rounded-xl font-bold hover:bg-[#c5a059] transition flex justify-center items-center gap-2 shadow-lg">
                    <Wrench size={18} /> ГҳВЁГҳВҜГҳВЎ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ (ГҳВЈГҷвҖ ГҳВ§ ГҷВҒГҷЕ  ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЛҶГҷвҖҡГҳВ№)
                  </button>
                )}

                {ticket.status === "ГҳВ¬ГҳВ§ГҳВұГҷЕ  ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖһ" && (
                  <div className="bg-green-50 p-4 rounded-xl border border-green-200 text-center animate-fadeIn">
                    <label className="block text-sm font-bold text-green-800 mb-2">ГҳВЈГҳВҜГҳВ®ГҷвҖһ ГҳВұГҷвҖҰГҳВІ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВҘГҳВәГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҷвҖҡ (OTP) ГҷвҖҰГҷвҖ  ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҷвҖҰГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ ГҷвҖһГҳВҘГҷвҖ ГҷвҖЎГҳВ§ГҳВЎ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷвҖЎГҷвҖҰГҳВ©</label>
                    <div className="flex gap-2">
                      <input 
                        type="text" maxLength={4} placeholder="----"
                        value={otpInputs[ticket.id] || ""}
                        onChange={(e) => setOtpInputs({...otpInputs, [ticket.id]: e.target.value})}
                        className="w-full text-center text-xl font-black p-3 rounded-xl border border-green-300 outline-none focus:border-green-500 tracking-widest"
                      />
                      <button onClick={() => handleOtpSubmit(ticket)} className="bg-green-600 text-white px-6 rounded-xl font-bold hover:bg-green-700 transition shadow-md">ГҳВҘГҳВәГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҷвҖҡ</button>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

// --- ГҳВЈГҳВҜГҳВ§ГҳВ© ГҷВҒГҳВӯГҳВө ГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҳВіГҳВӘГҷвҖһГҳВ§ГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷЛҶГҳВӯГҳВҜГҳВ§ГҳВӘ (ГҷвҖ ГҳВіГҳВ®ГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВ№ГҳВ§ГҷЕ ГҷЕ ГҳВұ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖЎГҷвҖ ГҳВҜГҳВіГҷЕ ГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҷЕ ГҳВ© ГҷЛҶГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВ®ГҳВөГҳВөГҳВ© ГҷвҖһГҷЖ’ГҷвҖһ ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒГҳВ©) ---
const UnitInspectionView = ({ user, showToast }) => {
  const [selectedUnit, setSelectedUnit] = useState("SM-A01");
  const [activeRoom, setActiveRoom] = useState("entrance");
  const [inspectionData, setInspectionData] = useState({});
  const [isSaving, setIsSaving] = useState(false);
  const [previewPlan, setPreviewPlan] = useState(null);

  const getUnitImage = (unit) => {
    const images = {
      "SM-A01": getImg("1_SOkisFdEjokohC6DwFjJAakT0DxJild"),
      "SM-A02": getImg("1_SOkisFdEjokohC6DwFjJAakT0DxJild"),
      "SM-A03": getImg("1o0NXJ_iC-LhrvDIC4i_uOy0WSfJfsAG1"),
      "SM-A04": getImg("1o0NXJ_iC-LhrvDIC4i_uOy0WSfJfsAG1"),
      "SM-A05": getImg("1MZuAEed1Vdn70eknds87xSInFEPINogE"),
      "SM-A06": getImg("1MZuAEed1Vdn70eknds87xSInFEPINogE"),
      "SM-A07": getImg("1dMNgoNkLMjmjOeHA1R98ApKOX8yFK1y1") 
    };
    return images[unit];
  };

  const getRoomsForUnit = (unit) => {
    const isRoof = unit === "SM-A07";
    return [
      { id: "entrance", label: "ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВҜГҳВ®ГҷвҖһ ГҷЛҶГҷвҖҰГҳВ¬ГҷвҖһГҳВі ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ¶ГҷЕ ГҷЛҶГҷВҒ", icon: DoorOpen },
      { id: "living", label: "ГҳВөГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВ№ГҷЕ ГҳВҙГҳВ©", icon: Sofa },
      { id: "kitchen", label: "ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВ·ГҳВЁГҳВ®", icon: ChefHat },
      { id: "master_bed", label: "ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖ ГҷЛҶГҷвҖҰ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВұГҳВҰГҷЕ ГҳВіГҷЕ ГҳВ©", icon: Bed },
      { id: "bed_2", label: "ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒГҳВ© ГҷвҖ ГҷЛҶГҷвҖҰ 2", icon: Bed },
      { id: "bed_3", label: "ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒГҳВ© ГҷвҖ ГҷЛҶГҷвҖҰ 3", icon: Bed },
      { id: "bed_4", label: "ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒГҳВ© ГҷвҖ ГҷЛҶГҷвҖҰ 4", icon: Bed },
      ...(isRoof ? [] : [{ id: "bed_5", label: "ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒГҳВ© ГҷвҖ ГҷЛҶГҷвҖҰ 5", icon: Bed }]),
      { id: "bath_1", label: "ГҳВҜГҷЛҶГҳВұГҳВ© ГҷвҖҰГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖЎ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ¶ГҷЕ ГҷЛҶГҷВҒ", icon: Bath },
      { id: "bath_2", label: "ГҳВҜГҷЛҶГҳВұГҳВ© ГҷвҖҰГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖЎ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ№ГҳВ§ГҳВҰГҷвҖһГҳВ©", icon: Bath },
      { id: "bath_3", label: "ГҳВҜГҷЛҶГҳВұГҳВ© ГҷвҖҰГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖЎ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҷвҖҰГҳВ§ГҳВіГҳВӘГҳВұ", icon: Bath },
      { id: "bath_4", label: "ГҳВҜГҷЛҶГҳВұГҳВ© ГҷвҖҰГҷЕ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖЎ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ®ГҳВ§ГҳВҜГҷвҖҰГҳВ©", icon: Bath },
      { id: "maid", label: "ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ®ГҳВ§ГҳВҜГҷвҖҰГҳВ©", icon: UserCheck },
      { id: "laundry", label: "ГҳВәГҳВұГҷВҒГҳВ© ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВәГҳВіГҷЕ ГҷвҖһ", icon: Droplets },
      ...(isRoof ? [{ id: "roof", label: "ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВіГҳВ·ГҳВӯ ГҳВ§ГҷвҖһГҳВ®ГҳВ§ГҳВө", icon: Umbrella }] : [])
    ];
  };
